Import Pandas¶

In [2]:
import pandas as pd

Read in the dataset¶

In [3]:
data = pd.read_csv('data-zillow.csv')

Get Mean price for every State¶

In [7]:
grouped_data = data[['State', 'Price']].groupby('State').mean()
